Hamilton</h2>\n    \n  \n  <div class=\"pane-content\">\n    <div class=\"region-gore-first\">\n  <div class=\"region-inner clearfix\">\n    \n<div class=\"pane-custom-coh-content\"><h3 class=\"pane-title\">Contact Centre</h3></div>\n  <h4 class=\"pane-custom-coh-title\">Phone</h4>\n\n<div class=\"pane-custom-coh-content\"><p>905-546-2489</p></div>\n  <h4 class=\"pane-custom-coh-title\">Email</h4>\n\n<div class=\"pane-custom-coh-content\"><p><a href=\"mailto:askCity@hamilton.ca\">askCity@hamilton.ca</a></p>\n</div>\n  <h4 class=\"pane-custom-coh-title\">Hours of Operation</h4>\n\n<div class=\"pane-custom-coh-content\"><p>Monday to Friday 8:30 am to 4:30 pm</p>\n<p class=\"pane-token-title\"><strong>Emergency After Hours Service</strong></p>\n\n<p>Monday to Friday 4:30 pm to 8:30 am and weekends.<br>\nCall for after hours emergencies involving roads, water mains, sewer systems, public health and safety issues.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"/city-initiatives/site-policies/contact-us\">More contact information</a></p>\n</div>\n  </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"region-gore-second\">\n  <div class=\"region-inner
